<tr>
<td class="noprint" colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><img alt="" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="33" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Soccerball_current_event.svg/33px-Soccerball_current_event.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Soccerball_current_event.svg/50px-Soccerball_current_event.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Soccerball_current_event.svg/66px-Soccerball_current_event.svg.png 2x" width="33"/> <i><a href="/wiki/2016_Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas_season" title="2016 Botafogo de Futebol e Regatas season">Current season</a></i></td>
</tr>
</table>
<p><b>Botafogo de Futebol e Regatas</b> (<small>Portuguese pronunciation: </small><span class="IPA" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA_for_Portuguese" title="Help:IPA for Portuguese">[bɔtaˈfoɡu dʒi futʃiˈbɔw i ʁeˈɡataʃ]</a></span>; <i>Botafogo Football and Regatta</i>), also known as <b>Botafogo</b> and familiarly as <i>A Estrela Solitária</i> (The Lone Star), is a <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> <a href="/wiki/Sports_club" title="Sports club">sports club</a> based in <a href="/wiki/Botafogo" title="Botafogo">Botafogo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Rio de Janeiro">Rio de Janeiro</a>. Although they compete in a number of different sports, Botafogo is mostly known for its <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">association football</a> team. It plays in the <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Carioca" title="Campeonato Carioca">Campeonato Carioca</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[nb 1]</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/States_of_Brazil" title="States of Brazil">state of</a> <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro_(state)" title="Rio de Janeiro (state)">Rio de Janeiro</a>'s premier <a href="/wiki/State_football_leagues_in_Brazil" title="State football leagues in Brazil">state league</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Brasileiro_S%C3%A9rie_A" title="Campeonato Brasileiro Série A">Brasileirão Série A</a>. It was appointed by <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> to the group of the biggest clubs in the twentieth century.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fifaum_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-fifaum-3">[2]</a></sup></p>
<p>In addition, the club has some of the top records of Brazilian football, as the largest number of unbeaten matches: 52 games between 1977 and 1978;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[3]</a></sup> the matches unbeaten record in the <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Brasileiro_S%C3%A9rie_A" title="Campeonato Brasileiro Série A">Brazilian Championship</a> games: 42, also between 1977 and 1978;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42jg_5-0"><a href="#cite_note-42jg-5">[4]</a></sup> the largest number of players participations in total matches of the <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil national football team</a> (considering official and unofficial games): 1,094 participations<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[5]</a></sup> and the largest number of players assigned to the Brazilian national team for <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">World Cup</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[6]</a></sup> The club is still responsible for the greatest victory ever recorded in Brazilian football: 24-0 against Sport Club Mangueira in 1909.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[7]</a></sup></p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Formation_and_merger">Formation and merger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Formation and merger">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On July 1, 1894, <b>Club de Regatas Botafogo</b> was founded.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[8]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Botafogo1906.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="329" data-file-width="531" height="136" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/Botafogo1906.jpg/220px-Botafogo1906.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/Botafogo1906.jpg/330px-Botafogo1906.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/Botafogo1906.jpg/440px-Botafogo1906.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Botafogo1906.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The 1906 <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> team.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>On August 12, 1904, another club was founded in the neighbourhood: the Electro Club, the name first given to the Botafogo Football Club. The idea came during an algebra lesson at Alfredo Gomes College, when Flávio Ramos wrote to his friend Emmanuel Sodré: "Itamar has a football club in Martins Ferreira Street. Let's establish another one, in Largo dos Leões, what do you think? We can speak to the Wernecks, to Arthur César, Vicente and Jacques". And so the Electro Club was founded. But this name wouldn't last. After a suggestion from Dona Chiquitota, Flávio's grandmother, the club finally became the Botafogo Football Club, on September 18 of the same year. The colours? Black and white., just like <i>Juventus FC</i>, the team of Itamar Tavares, one of the club's founders. And the badge, drawn by Basílio Vianna Jr., in Swiss style with the BFC monogram. The Botafogo Football Club would soon become one of the strongest football teams in <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Rio de Janeiro">Rio de Janeiro</a>, winning the championships of 1907, 1910, 1912 and more.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gazetaesportivaelectrobotafogo_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-gazetaesportivaelectrobotafogo-10">[9]</a></sup></p>
<p>The same name, the same location, the same colours and the most important thing: the same supporters. It seemed that the destiny of both clubs was to become one. And so it happened: on December 8, 1942 they finally merged. It was after a basketball match between both clubs, when Botafogo Football Club player Armando Albano died suddenly, that the idea began to become truth. At the tragic occasion, the president of Club de Regatas Botafogo, Augusto Frederico Schmidt (also a major Brazilian poet) spoke: "At this time, I declare to Albano that his last match ended with the victory of his team. We won't play no longer the time left on the clock. We all want the young fighter to leave this great night as a winner. This is how we salute him". Eduardo Góis Trindade, Botafogo Football Club's president said: "Between the matches of our clubs, only one can be the winner: Botafogo!". And then Schmidt declared the fusion: "What else do we need to our clubs become one?". And so they did: Botafogo de Futebol e Regatas finally became true. The Football Club's badge became black, and the monogram substituted by Clube de Regatas' lone star.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-history1942_11-0"><a href="#cite_note-history1942-11">[10]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="On_the_field">On the field</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: On the field">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Time_Botafogo_1907.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="372" data-file-width="450" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Time_Botafogo_1907.jpg/200px-Time_Botafogo_1907.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Time_Botafogo_1907.jpg/300px-Time_Botafogo_1907.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Time_Botafogo_1907.jpg/400px-Time_Botafogo_1907.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Time_Botafogo_1907.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The team that won its first <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Carioca" title="Campeonato Carioca">Campeonato Carioca</a> in 1907.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Time_Botafogo_1910.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="348" data-file-width="531" height="164" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Time_Botafogo_1910.jpg/250px-Time_Botafogo_1910.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Time_Botafogo_1910.jpg/375px-Time_Botafogo_1910.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Time_Botafogo_1910.jpg/500px-Time_Botafogo_1910.jpg 2x" width="250"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Time_Botafogo_1910.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The team of 1910.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The team won the <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Carioca" title="Campeonato Carioca">Campeonato Carioca</a> in 1907, 1910 and 1912. In 1909 the team beat <a href="/wiki/Sport_Club_Mangueira" title="Sport Club Mangueira">Mangueira</a> 24–0, which remains the highest score in Brazilian football. They won further state titles in 1930, 1932, 1933, 1934 and 1935.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[11]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Botafogo_1930.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="363" data-file-width="525" height="173" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Botafogo_1930.jpg/250px-Botafogo_1930.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Botafogo_1930.jpg/375px-Botafogo_1930.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Botafogo_1930.jpg/500px-Botafogo_1930.jpg 2x" width="250"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Botafogo_1930.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
In 1930 Botafogo won its 4th. Carioca title.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In the 1940s, after the creation of "Botafogo de Futebol e Regatas", the best player of the team was <a href="/wiki/Heleno_de_Freitas" title="Heleno de Freitas">Heleno de Freitas</a>. However, Heleno did not win a championship for Botafogo. He scored 204 goals in 233 matches but went to <a href="/wiki/Boca_Juniors" title="Boca Juniors">Boca Juniors</a> in 1948, the year Botafogo won its 9th state championship.</p>
<p>They won the <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Carioca" title="Campeonato Carioca">Campeonato Carioca</a> in 1957, 1961 and 1962, and in 1968 they won <a href="/wiki/Ta%C3%A7a_Brasil" title="Taça Brasil">Serie A</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-swaytroph_13-0"><a href="#cite_note-swaytroph-13">[12]</a></sup></p>
<p>1989 ended a period of 21 years without a title when the club won the state championship, retaining the trophy in 1990.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-swaytroph_13-1"><a href="#cite_note-swaytroph-13">[12]</a></sup></p>
<p>In the 1990s, Botafogo won <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Copa_Conmebol" title="Copa Conmebol">Copa Conmebol</a> (the precursor of the current <a href="/wiki/Copa_Sudamericana" title="Copa Sudamericana">Copa Sudamericana</a>)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[13]</a></sup></p>
<p>Botafogo would be relegated to the Second Division after ranking last in the Brazilian League of 2002. In 2003, Botafogo ranked second in Brazil's Second division (after <a href="/wiki/Sociedade_Esportiva_Palmeiras" title="Sociedade Esportiva Palmeiras">Palmeiras</a>) and returned to the First Division.</p>
<p>In 2006, the club won for the 18th time the Rio de Janeiro State Championship. Nowadays, Botafogo is the only club to win titles in three different centuries, including the state championship of rowing in 1899.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Stadium">Stadium</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Stadium">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Est%C3%A1dio_da_Rua_Volunt%C3%A1rios_da_P%C3%A1tria_(1909).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="359" data-file-width="500" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Est%C3%A1dio_da_Rua_Volunt%C3%A1rios_da_P%C3%A1tria_%281909%29.jpg/230px-Est%C3%A1dio_da_Rua_Volunt%C3%A1rios_da_P%C3%A1tria_%281909%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Est%C3%A1dio_da_Rua_Volunt%C3%A1rios_da_P%C3%A1tria_%281909%29.jpg/345px-Est%C3%A1dio_da_Rua_Volunt%C3%A1rios_da_P%C3%A1tria_%281909%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Est%C3%A1dio_da_Rua_Volunt%C3%A1rios_da_P%C3%A1tria_%281909%29.jpg/460px-Est%C3%A1dio_da_Rua_Volunt%C3%A1rios_da_P%C3%A1tria_%281909%29.jpg 2x" width="230"/></a>

</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:General_Severiano.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1536" data-file-width="2048" height="173" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/General_Severiano.JPG/230px-General_Severiano.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/General_Severiano.JPG/345px-General_Severiano.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/General_Severiano.JPG/460px-General_Severiano.JPG 2x" width="230"/></a>

</div>
<p>Their home ground is the <a href="/wiki/Est%C3%A1dio_Ol%C3%ADmpico_Jo%C3%A3o_Havelange" title="Estádio Olímpico João Havelange">Estádio Olímpico João Havelange</a>, which is known as the Estádio Nilton Santos for Botafogo matches.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[14]</a></sup></p>
<div class="center">
<div class="thumb tnone">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:502px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Stitched_003.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="587" data-file-width="1600" height="183" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Stitched_003.jpg/500px-Stitched_003.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Stitched_003.jpg/750px-Stitched_003.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Stitched_003.jpg/1000px-Stitched_003.jpg 2x" width="500"/></a>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Rivals">Rivals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Rivals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Its biggest rivals are from the same city: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fluminense_Football_Club" title="Fluminense Football Club">Fluminense</a>, <a href="/wiki/Clube_de_Regatas_do_Flamengo" title="Clube de Regatas do Flamengo">Flamengo</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Club_de_Regatas_Vasco_da_Gama" title="Club de Regatas Vasco da Gama">Vasco da Gama</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Symbols">Symbols</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Symbols">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bota_badges.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="375" data-file-width="240" height="266" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/8c/Bota_badges.jpg/170px-Bota_badges.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/8/8c/Bota_badges.jpg 1.5x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Bota_badges.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Historical badges.</div>
</div>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lone_Star">Lone Star</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Lone Star">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Lone <a href="/wiki/Star" title="Star">Star</a> (<i>Estrela Solitária</i>) is currently present in Botafogo's flag and crest. This star was the principal symbol of Club de Regatas Botafogo. After the two Botafogos merged, the Lone Star became one of the most important symbols of Botafogo's <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> team.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Flag">Flag</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Flag">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The old <a href="/wiki/Flag" title="Flag">flag</a> of Club de Regatas Botafogo was white with a small black square which contained the Lone Star. The Football Club had a flag with nine black and white stripes with the club's crest localized in the center. Botafogo de Futebol e Regatas then based its flag on the two old clubs. The flag has five black and four white stripes, with a black square at the upper left side with the Lone Star.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2014)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Uniform">Uniform</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Uniform">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Their primary uniform consists of a black jersey with vertical white stripes, black shorts and grey socks. Their secondary uniform is all white. An all black uniform may also be used. The socks, although traditionally grey, may also be black or even white on rare occasions.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Mascots">Mascots</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Mascots">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:162px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Manequinho_2.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1677" data-file-width="1485" height="181" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Manequinho_2.JPG/160px-Manequinho_2.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Manequinho_2.JPG/240px-Manequinho_2.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Manequinho_2.JPG/320px-Manequinho_2.JPG 2x" width="160"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Manequinho_2.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
"Manequinho", the mascot of the club.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In 1948 a stray dog named <i>Biriba</i>, known for urinating on the players, was the mascot that led them to the Campeonato Carioca.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[15]</a></sup> For some time before the adoption of <i>Manequinho</i> as mascot, Botafogo had <a href="/wiki/Donald_Duck" title="Donald Duck">Donald Duck</a> as their mascot, associated with the team fans' fiery temper (as well as, notoriously, 1940s idol <a href="/wiki/Heleno_de_Freitas" title="Heleno de Freitas">Heleno de Freitas</a>). Due to image rights problems with the Walt Disney Company, Donald did not become an official mascot.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Financial_situation">Financial situation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Financial situation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In 2006 Botafogo had <i>Supergasbras</i> and <i>Alê</i> as sponsors, the arrangement during that year earned the team $3.2 million (R$7.2 million).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-esportes.terra.com.br_17-0"><a href="#cite_note-esportes.terra.com.br-17">[16]</a></sup> The next year, Botafogo managed to sign the sixth highest sponsorship deal in Brazil<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[17]</a></sup> the new sponsor <i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Liquig%C3%A1s&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Liquigás (page does not exist)">Liquigás</a></i>, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Petrobr%C3%A1s" title="Petrobrás">Petrobrás</a> subsidiary paid the club $3.9 million (R$7.8 million) under the terms of the 1-year contract.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-esportes.terra.com.br_17-1"><a href="#cite_note-esportes.terra.com.br-17">[16]</a></sup> In 2008 not only the agreement with <i>Liquigás</i> was renewed for another year but it also became more lucrative since the sponsorship was raised to around $5 million (R$10.2 million).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[18]</a></sup></p>
<p>Botafogo generated in 2007 the 12th biggest <a href="/wiki/Revenue" title="Revenue">revenue</a> for all Brazilian Football clubs, that year's revenues totalled $20.8 million (or R$41.1 million) but Botafogo had a net loss of $1.9 million (or R$3.7 million).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[19]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[20]</a></sup> Also at the end of 2007 Botafogo had total <a href="/wiki/Debt" title="Debt">debts</a> of $106.1 million (or R$209.7 million).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[21]</a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Records">Records</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Records">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Golden Ball winners:</p>

</ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Managers">Managers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Managers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2015)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>

<tr>
<td style="width: 33.33%;text-align:left;vertical-align:top;">
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil"><img alt="Brazil" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="504" data-file-width="720" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/22px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/33px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/43px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 2x" width="22"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Carvalho_Leite" title="Carvalho Leite">Carvalho Leite</a> (1941–42), (1942–43)</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil"><img alt="Brazil" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="504" data-file-width="720" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/22px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/33px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/43px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 2x" width="22"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Martim_M%C3%A9rcio_da_Silveira" title="Martim Mércio da Silveira">Martim Silveira</a> (1944), (1946)</li>
